</header><div class="entry-content"><div class="tasty-pins-hidden-image-container" style="display:none;"><img alt="Wooden spoon resting in a pot of Curried Cauliflower Soup" class="tasty-pins-hidden-image" data-pin-description="COMFORTING Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup! 1 Pot, simple ingredients, SO nourishing! #plantbased #glutenfree #grainfree #soup #minimalistbaker #recipe" data-pin-media="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/MB-CurriedCauliflowerSoup-Pinterest.jpg" data-pin-title="Creamy Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup (1 Pot!)" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/MB-CurriedCauliflowerSoup-Pinterest-200x200.jpg"/></div>
<input class="jpibfi" type="hidden"/>

<p>This soup is our last recipe of 2019! We couldn’t think of a better final dish to share than a comforting, warm hug in the form of creamy soup in the midst of winter.</p>
<p>This <strong>1-pot soup</strong> is a blend of red lentils, ginger, spices, carrots, and cauliflower, making it full of fiber and plant-based protein and <em>big</em> on flavor. Let us show you how it’s done!</p>
<iframe allow="accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="380" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/R1lVkJXudxE" width="680"></iframe>

1 Pot, simple ingredients, SO nourishing! #plantbased #glutenfree #grainfree #soup #minimalistbaker #recipe" data-pin-title="Creamy Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup (1 Pot!)" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-222x300.jpg 222w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-768x1040.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-756x1024.jpg 756w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-600x812.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-680x921.jpg 680w"/></figure>
<span id="more-48787"></span>
<p>This soup starts with sautéing onion, garlic, ginger, and carrot. Then add cauliflower, broth, and lentils.</p>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Using a wooden spoon to stir oninos, carrot, celery, and garlic for our Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup recipe" class="wp-image-48805" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Creamy Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup (1 Pot!)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-curried-cauliflower-lentil-soup-1-pot/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-3.jpg" data-pin-description="COMFORTING Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup! 1 Pot, simple ingredients, SO nourishing! #plantbased #glutenfree #grainfree #soup #minimalistbaker #recipe" data-pin-title="Creamy Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup (1 Pot!)" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-3.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-3.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-3-202x300.jpg 202w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-3-768x1139.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-3-691x1024.jpg 691w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-3-600x890.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-3-680x1008.jpg 680w"/></figure>
<p>For spices, we kept things simple with fresh ginger, <a aria-label="curry powder (opens in a new tab)" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/diy-curry-powder/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">curry powder</a>, and a pinch of cayenne, which complements the sweetness of the carrots beautifully. </p>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Using an immersion blender to make Creamy Curried Cauliflower Soup" class="wp-image-48809" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Creamy Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup (1 Pot!)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-curried-cauliflower-lentil-soup-1-pot/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-14.jpg" data-pin-description="COMFORTING Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup! 1 Pot, simple ingredients, SO nourishing! #plantbased #glutenfree #grainfree #soup #minimalistbaker #recipe" data-pin-title="Creamy Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup (1 Pot!)" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-14.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-14.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-14-203x300.jpg 203w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-14-768x1136.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-14-692x1024.jpg 692w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-14-600x888.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-14-680x1006.jpg 680w"/></figure>
<p>A touch of coconut milk before blending makes for the <em>ultimate</em> creamy texture. Swoon!</p>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Holding a pot of Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup" class="wp-image-48816" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Creamy Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup (1 Pot!)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-curried-cauliflower-lentil-soup-1-pot/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/COMFORTING-Curried-Cauliflower-Lentil-Soup-1-Pot-simple-ingredients-SO-nourishing-plantbased-glutenfree-grainfree-soup-minimalistbaker-recipe-27.jpg" data-pin-description="COMFORTING Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup! <p>We hope you LOVE this soup! It’s:</p>
<ul><li>Creamy</li><li>Comforting</li><li>Nutrient-rich</li><li>Quick &amp; easy to make</li><li>Versatile</li><li>&amp; Delicious</li></ul>
<p>This would make the <em>perfect</em> weeknight soup when you need something nourishing on the table fast. It’s delicious on its own, but would also pair well with our <a aria-label="Apple Pecan Arugula Salad (opens in a new tab)" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/apple-pecan-arugula-salad/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Apple Pecan Arugula Salad</a>, <a aria-label="Easy Whole Grain Flatbread (opens in a new tab)" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/garlic-herb-flatbread/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Garlic Herb Flatbread</a> (or <a aria-label="Naan (opens in a new tab)" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/easy-vegan-naan/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Naan</a>), or our <a aria-label="Easy Marinated Grilled Chicken (opens in a new tab)" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/easy-marinated-grilled-chicken-30-minutes/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Easy Marinated Grilled Chicken</a>. </p>
<p><strong>Bonus</strong>: It reheats beautifully, making it ideal for leftovers, lunches, and freezer meals!</p>

<h2 class="wprm-recipe-name">Creamy Curried Cauliflower Lentil Soup (1 Pot!)</h2>
<div class="wprm-recipe-summary">
<p>Creamy, 1-pot curried cauliflower soup with carrots, ginger, and red lentils! Subtly spiced, quick and easy to make, and perfect for meal prep!</p> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-author-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-author-name">Author:</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-author">Minimalist Baker</span>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-times-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-prep-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-prep-time-name">Prep Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-prep_time wprm-recipe-prep_time-minutes">10</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-prep_time-unit wprm-recipe-prep_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-cook-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-cook-time-name">Cook Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-cook_time wprm-recipe-cook_time-minutes">30</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-cook_time-unit wprm-recipe-cook_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-total-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-total-time-name">Total Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-total_time wprm-recipe-total_time-minutes">40</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-total_time-unit wprm-recipe-total_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-servings-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-servings-name">Servings:</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-servings">4</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-servings-unit">(Servings)</span>

					3-4 Days				</span>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredients-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Ingredients</h3>
<div class="wprm-unit-conversion-container"><a class="wprm-unit-conversion wprmpuc-active" data-recipe="48927" data-system="1" href="#">US Customary</a> – <a class="wprm-unit-conversion" data-recipe="48927" data-system="2" href="#">Metric</a></div> <div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">avocado oil </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub water for oil-free)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">medium</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">white or yellow onion</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">medium</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">carrots, diced</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">stalk</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">celery, diced </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(<em><strong>optional</strong></em>)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1 ½</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">minced fresh ginger</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2-3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cloves</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">garlic, minced</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">head</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">cauliflower, cut into bite-size pieces </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(~4 cups as original recipe is written)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2-3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/diy-curry-powder/" target="_blank">curry powder</a></span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">pinch</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">cayenne</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(<em><strong>optional</strong></em>)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cups</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/easy-1-pot-vegetable-broth/" target="_blank">vegetable broth</a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/how-to-make-bone-broth/" target="_blank">chicken broth</a> if not vegan or vegetarian)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">red lentils</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">sea salt, plus more to taste</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">coconut cream </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub 1/4 cup full-fat coconut milk as the recipe is written // adjust amount if altering serving size)</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Instructions</h3>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group">
<ol class="wprm-recipe-instructions">
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Heat a large pot (or <a href="https://aax-us-east.amazon-adsystem.com/x/c/Qi62CGytC1d6HG4IxA3VLxMAAAFuTXHnXwEAAAFKATewzFQ/https://www.amazon.com/dp/B01BFFU28I/?creativeASIN=B01BFFU28I&amp;linkCode=w61&amp;imprToken=v7la9BNDiVMbYHJb87Oolg&amp;slotNum=3&amp;tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Dutch oven</a>) over medium heat. Once hot, add oil, onion, carrots, and celery (optional) and sauté for 4-5 minutes — stirring occasionally. Then add ginger and garlic and sauté for 2-3 minutes more or until fragrant.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Add cauliflower, curry powder, cayenne (optional), broth, lentils, and salt. Bring to a low boil over medium heat and then reduce heat to low, cover, and simmer for 15 minutes or until lentils and cauliflower are tender.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Add coconut cream and blend with an <a href="https://aax-us-east.amazon-adsystem.com/x/c/Qsvwq-AkDkq3_2Y5hxh_4aQAAAFuTYiblQEAAAFKAUPP7vA/https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B005MMNAYE/ref=?creativeASIN=B005MMNAYE&amp;linkCode=w61&amp;imprToken=7Az2Yh67o0k9T5TdqSE-pw&amp;slotNum=21&amp;tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">immersion blender</a> until creamy and no bits remain (if it has trouble blending, you can optionally transfer to a <a href="https://aax-us-east.amazon-adsystem.com/x/c/QrXL9OzdNZbC1R-PlCgcTXEAAAFvJEJy1AEAAAFKAXsw-Ws/https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B008H4SLV6/?creativeASIN=B008H4SLV6&amp;linkCode=w61&amp;imprToken=663jPIfJ83hFY3P1cWkoKQ&amp;slotNum=13" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">blender</a> and blend on high until creamy and smooth). </p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Taste and adjust seasonings, adding more curry powder for spice, cayenne for heat, or salt for overall flavor. Continue cooking for a few more minutes over medium heat.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Serve as is or with garnish of choice (we went with fresh cilantro and an additional swirl of coconut milk). Store leftovers covered in the refrigerator for 3-4 days or in the freezer up to 1 month. </p></div>
</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-864675">
<article id="article-comment-864675">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Barbara S Stoddard" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/aad4932c4d24f09ab06b029e6f83b1f1?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/aad4932c4d24f09ab06b029e6f83b1f1?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Barbara S Stoddard" width="96"><span itemprop="name">Barbara S Stoddard</span> <span class="says">says</span> </img></p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-curried-cauliflower-lentil-soup-1-pot/?t=1582413311#comment-864675">February 19, 2020 at 8:43 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This has been my go-to recipe all winter.  I make it every week and the amount is perfect for two people with a few leftover meals.  The first time I made it I didn’t puree it. It was good, but even better once I used my immersion blender: smooth, creamy and richly flavored.  Instead of the coconut cream I use 1/2 can of full fat coconut milk.  I made it for my bookclub last night and they all loved it.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Delicious!  I used the celery because I love it and I shook a few shakes of cayenne.  It was not overwhelmingly hot, but left a nice burn on my lips.  Bravo, great recipe!  Oh, I did use chicken broth and added an extra cup, as it was rather thick.  I will definitely make this again.</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-curried-cauliflower-lentil-soup-1-pot/?t=1582413311#comment-856316">January 18, 2020 at 8:04 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>My husband made this and we loved it. It is a keeper. He doubled it so we froze some.  We used low sodium / no sodium added vegetable broth and the coconut milk option. He doubled the ginger because we love it, and he also put spinach and a couple of broccoli crowns we had to use up. He blended half very smooth and the rest not as smooth so there were tiny chunks of the ginger. We also used some very hot smoked pepper powder we made this summer from our garden, it added a little kick if you like that. Yum! Thank MB!</p>

<img alt="Avatar for Merry Soellner" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a42077f4a5e49e00d65bc0824c2e34a4?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a42077f4a5e49e00d65bc0824c2e34a4?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Merry Soellner" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Merry Soellner</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-curried-cauliflower-lentil-soup-1-pot/?t=1582413311#comment-854735">January 9, 2020 at 12:10 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Super easy and delicious!  Especially nice on a cold winter night, with crusty bread.  All ingredients are available at just about any grocery.  I put a little too much cayenne in for most people, but I really love spice!  Would make a wonderful 1st course of a nice dinner, too.  It’s a little more unusual than a lot of the soup courses I’ve seen.</p>
<p>Again, delish!  Try it!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>This soup is so yummy! I made it last night, pretty much as the recipe called for (with slightly more lentils). I was actually surprised how flavourful it was! (Cauliflower can sometimes end up really bland). I blended 90% of it in my Vitamix and left the other 10% chunky. Soooo thick and delicious! Ate it for lunch with a little leftover basmati rice. Perfect winter meal!</p>

<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Lauren" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/1c36a1dff6ad28e21bb2488748ff994b?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/1c36a1dff6ad28e21bb2488748ff994b?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Lauren" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Lauren</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-curried-cauliflower-lentil-soup-1-pot/?t=1582413311#comment-854225">January 6, 2020 at 12:56 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I used brown lentils instead of red so the color was a little drab, but once I served this, people ate it right up and only had good things to say.  I have to say, the flavor the first night of serving it did not pack a punch (in my opinion), but I let it sit in the fridge for 2 days, the flavor frew, and it was delicious. Super easy to make. I love that it was in one pot. I did not use coconut cream, but light coconut milk. I added sour cream to mine because the light coconut milk was not as creamy as I wanted it (this was the first night). I did not add anything to the soup when I had it for left overs.</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-curried-cauliflower-lentil-soup-1-pot/?t=1582413311#comment-854151">January 6, 2020 at 11:06 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I accidentally used thai curry paste instead of curry powder, so it had a very thai taste. It was still good. I added more coconut cream than the recipe calls for, and I didn’t have celery. I cooked this in an instant pot for 3 minutes with quick release. I added coconut cream after I cooked it so that it would not burn.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Great weeknight recipe.  I used frozen cauliflower and the instant pot for a quick dinner.  Threw in some spinach at the end.  Thanks for another fantastic recipe!</p>

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-853575">
<article id="article-comment-853575">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Rachel" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/285f53864bb068e01614b89154f771f2?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/285f53864bb068e01614b89154f771f2?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Rachel" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Rachel</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-curried-cauliflower-lentil-soup-1-pot/?t=1582413311#comment-853575">January 2, 2020 at 7:06 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This was yummy! I made it with almost twice the lentils, found it a little bland and ended up doubling the ginger, curry powder, salt, and coconut milk and adding a hit of Sriracha. It’s not a dinner party soup, it’s a winter sick day soup–warm, nourishing, and humble. I served it with cilantro and pepitas to dress it up a little. I would make this again for the right mood.</p>
<div class="wprm-comment-rating">

<div class="comment-content">
<p>I am on a salt-restricted diet so used low salt veggie broth and just a pinch of salt. The soup is good and felt comforting on a cold Chicago New Years Eve but it needs more to replace the salt.  I’m no cook but wondered if turmeric might make it more flavorful? What else? I will make again for sure.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>This was great even though I only had 2c of veg broth and had to sub water for the rest! I omitted the cayenne so it wouldn’t be too spicy for the tiny human, and just added sriracha to mine for a bit of bite. Another easy and excellent recipe for grown ups that’s also 4-year old approved! Thanks!</p>

<p>I just made this for dinner tonight. I didn’t have the exact ingredients on hand so I used olive oil, organic Imagine Brand low sodium No-Chicken Broth (only 140 mg sodium per cup), light coconut milk, and red pepper flakes.  Then topped it with roasted pepitas and cilantro. It was very flavorful. Loved it &amp; looking forward to left overs tomorrow. So easy to make!</p>

<p>Hi Tracey, we used this <a href="https://aax-us-east.amazon-adsystem.com/x/c/QmTrk7AndYeGh9Ta8p04yWEAAAFvWDZ_uwEAAAFKAUSUBq4/https://www.amazon.com/dp/B01BFFU28I/?creativeASIN=B01BFFU28I&amp;linkCode=w61&amp;imprToken=Oc.DEML8fmBJ3J9fYCUshA&amp;slotNum=41&amp;tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="noopener nofollow noreferrer" target="_blank">Dutch oven</a>. The blade of the immersion blender doesn’t touch the bottom of the pan so we didn’t have any issues.</p>

				jQuery(document).ready(function () {

					function mgclInit() {
						if (jQuery.fn.off) {
							jQuery('.no-lightbox, .no-lightbox img').off('click'); // jQuery 1.7+
						}
						else {
							jQuery('.no-lightbox, .no-lightbox img').unbind('click'); // < jQuery 1.7
						}
						jQuery('a.no-lightbox').click(mgclOnClick);

						if (jQuery.fn.off) {
							jQuery('a.set-target').off('click'); // jQuery 1.7+
						}
						else {
							jQuery('a.set-target').unbind('click'); // < jQuery 1.7
						}
						jQuery('a.set-target').click(mgclOnClick);
					}

					function mgclOnClick() {
						if (!this.target || this.target == '' || this.target == '_self')
							window.location = this.href;
						else
							window.open(this.href,this.target);
						return false;
					}

					// From WP Gallery Custom Links
					// Reduce the number of  conflicting lightboxes
					function mgclAddLoadEvent(func) {
						var oldOnload = window.onload;
						if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
							window.onload = func;
						} else {
							window.onload = function() {
								oldOnload();
								func();
							}
						}
					}

					mgclAddLoadEvent(mgclInit);
					mgclInit();

				});
